Algorithms

Generative adversarial networks  
I. Goodfellow \+7  
Communications of the ACM  
2014 ·  
29,310 citations  
PDF  
DOI

The main algorithm introduced and studied in this paper is the Generative Adversarial Network (GAN) algorithm. The paper provides a detailed description of the GAN algorithm, including the training procedure (Algorithm 1\) and the theoretical analysis of the algorithm.

Denoising Diffusion Probabilistic Models  
Jonathan Ho \+2  
Neural Information Processing Systems  
2020 ·  
12,917 citations

1\. Diffusion probabilistic models, a class of latent variable models inspired by nonequilibrium thermodynamics  
2\. A novel connection between diffusion probabilistic models and denoising score matching with Langevin dynamics  
3\. A weighted variational bound used for training the diffusion models  
4\. A progressive lossy decompression scheme that generalizes autoregressive decoding

High-Resolution Image Synthesis with Latent Diffusion Models  
Robin Rombach \+4  
Computer Vision and Pattern Recognition  
2021 ·  
11,685 citations  
DOI

1\) Diffusion models (DMs) for image synthesis  
2\) Latent diffusion models (LDMs), which apply DMs in the latent space of pretrained autoencoders  
3\) Cross-attention layers incorporated into the diffusion model architecture to enable flexible conditioning and high-resolution synthesis

Photo-Realistic Single Image Super-Resolution Using a Generative Adversarial Network  
C. Ledig \+8  
Computer Vision and Pattern Recognition  
2016 ·  
10,069 citations  
DOI

1\. SRGAN: A generative adversarial network (GAN) for single image super-resolution  
2\. Perceptual loss function: A loss function that combines an adversarial loss and a content loss based on perceptual similarity  
3\. Deep residual network: A deep neural network architecture used to recover photo-realistic textures from low-resolution input images

A Style-Based Generator Architecture for Generative Adversarial Networks  
Tero Karras \+2  
Computer Vision and Pattern Recognition  
2018 ·  
9,491 citations  
DOI

1\. A new generator architecture for generative adversarial networks (GANs) that borrows from style transfer literature.  
2\. Techniques to automatically learn an unsupervised separation of high-level attributes (e.g., pose, identity) and stochastic variation (e.g., freckles, hair) in the generated images.  
3\. Methods to enable intuitive, scale-specific control of the image synthesis.  
4\. Two new automated methods to quantify interpolation quality and disentanglement of the latent factors of variation, which can be applied to any generator architecture.

Accelerating the Super-Resolution Convolutional Neural Network  
Chao Dong \+2  
European Conference on Computer Vision  
2016 ·  
2,798 citations  
PDF  
DOI

1\. Use of a deconvolution layer at the end of the network to learn a direct mapping from low-resolution to high-resolution images without interpolation.  
2\. Reformulation of the mapping layer to first shrink the input feature dimension before mapping, and then expand it back afterwards.  
3\. Use of smaller filter sizes but more mapping layers in the network architecture.

DOI

The specific algorithms that were introduced, studied, or used in the E. Agustsson and R. Timofte (2017) study are the super-resolution algorithms submitted to the NTIRE 2017 challenge, which the paper compares to other representative methods from the literature. The paper does not provide the names or details of the specific algorithms, but it evaluates their performance on the DIV2K dataset and several other popular benchmark datasets.

A Neural Algorithm of Artistic Style  
Leon A. Gatys \+2  
arXiv.org  
2015 ·  
2,712 citations  
PDF  
DOI

1\. A content representation algorithm that extracts the high-level content information from an image using the feature responses in higher layers of a convolutional neural network (CNN).  
2\. A style representation algorithm that captures the texture and appearance information of an image using the correlations between the filter responses in different layers of the CNN.

3\) Incorporating additional affine transformations to accommodate local shape variations

2022 ·  
2,131 citations  
DOI

1\) A fine-tuning approach that takes a few images of a subject and binds a unique identifier to that subject in a pre-trained text-to-image diffusion model.  
2\) A new "autogenous class-specific prior preservation loss" that is used as part of the fine-tuning process to enable synthesizing the subject in diverse contexts.  
3\) Application of the DreamBooth approach to new tasks like subject recontextualization, text-guided view synthesis, and artistic rendering.

2021 ·  
1,465 citations  
DOI

IEEE Transactions on Pattern Analysis and Machine Intelligence  
2009 ·  
1,183 citations  
DOI

The key algorithm introduced and studied in this paper is a "geometric-flow-based" algorithm for computing superpixels that respects image boundaries while enforcing a compactness constraint to limit undersegmentation. This algorithm is described as being very fast, with a complexity that is approximately linear in image size.

The paper reviews deep learning algorithms for single image super-resolution (SISR), focusing on two key aspects: (1) efficient neural network architectures for SISR, and (2) effective optimization objectives for deep SISR learning. The paper does not provide the names of the specific deep learning algorithms reviewed, but rather discusses how these algorithms address limitations of baseline SISR methods.

SEEDS: Superpixels Extracted Via Energy-Driven Sampling  
M. Bergh \+4

2012 ·

PDF  
DOI

The specific algorithm introduced and studied in this paper is the SEEDS (Superpixels Extracted via Energy-Driven Sampling) algorithm, which uses a hill-climbing optimization approach to refine an initial superpixel partitioning by modifying the superpixel boundaries based on an energy function that enforces color similarity.

arXiv.org  
2022 ·  
581 citations  
DOI

3\. BEiT-3: A general-purpose multimodal foundation model built upon the Multiway Transformer architecture and Imglish pretraining, which achieves state-of-the-art performance on a wide range of vision and vision-language tasks.

PULSE: Self-Supervised Photo Upsampling via Latent Space Exploration of Generative Models  
Sachit Menon \+4  
Computer Vision and Pattern Recognition  
2020 ·  
508 citations  
PDF  
DOI

1\) A self-supervised super-resolution method that uses a pre-trained generative model, such as a GAN, to explore the latent space and find realistic high-resolution images that downscale correctly to the input low-resolution image.  
2\) A novel method for searching the latent space of the generative model by constraining the search to the surface of a hypersphere in the high-dimensional latent space, ensuring that the generated images remain realistic.  
3\) A "downscaling loss" function that penalizes the generated high-resolution images for not downscaling correctly to the input low-resolution image.

1\) An energy minimization framework for generating superpixels  
2\) Graph cuts optimization to minimize the energy function

Haochen Wang \+4

2022 ·  
450 citations  
DOI

1\. Score Jacobian Chaining: Applying the chain rule to backpropagate the score (gradient) of a 2D diffusion model through the Jacobian of a differentiable 3D renderer (voxel radiance field) to generate 3D data.  
2\. Novel estimation mechanism: A technique proposed by the authors to resolve the distribution mismatch challenge that arises when applying a 2D diffusion model to 3D generation.

Fusion of multi-exposure images  
A. Goshtasby  
Image and Vision Computing  
2005 ·  
311 citations  
DOI

1\. A method for fusing multiple exposure images of a static scene taken by a stationary camera into a single image with maximum information content.  
2\. Partitioning the image domain into uniform blocks and selecting the image with the most information in each block.  
3\. Blending the selected images using monotonically decreasing blending functions centered on the blocks with a sum of 1 across the image domain.  
4\. Using a gradient-ascent algorithm to determine the optimal block size and blending function width to maximize the information content in the final fused image.

Shap-E: Generating Conditional 3D Implicit Functions  
Heewoo Jun \+1  
arXiv.org  
2023 ·  
248 citations  
DOI

1\. A conditional generative model that generates the parameters of implicit functions for 3D assets, allowing for the generation of multiple output representations (textured meshes and neural radiance fields).  
2\. A two-stage training process, where first an encoder is trained to map 3D assets into the parameters of an implicit function, and then a conditional diffusion model is trained on the outputs of the encoder.  
3\. A comparison to the Point-E model, an explicit generative model over point clouds, showing that Shap-E converges faster and reaches comparable or better sample quality despite modeling a higher-dimensional, multi-representation output space.

2016 ·  
235 citations

The key algorithm introduced in this paper is the "LR-GAN" (Layered Recursive Generative Adversarial Network) model, which is a generative adversarial network (GAN) that generates images by separately and recursively generating the background and foreground, and then stitching them together in a contextually relevant manner. For each foreground object, the model learns to generate its appearance, shape, and pose.

Illiterate DALL-E Learns to Compose  
Gautam Singh \+2  
International Conference on Learning Representations  
2021 ·  
118 citations

1\) DALL-E: A text-to-image generation model that uses text prompts to achieve systematic generalization in image composition.  
2\) Slot Attention model: An object-centric representation model that can learn composable representations without text prompts, but has limited ability for systematic generalization in zero-shot generation.  
3\) SLATE (Slot-based Autoencoding): A novel slot-based autoencoding architecture proposed in this paper that combines the strengths of DALL-E and Slot Attention models to achieve systematic generalization in zero-shot image generation without text prompts.  
4\) Image GPT decoder conditioned on slots: A decoder used in the SLATE model to capture complex interactions between the slots and pixels, in contrast to the pixel-mixture decoders used in existing object-centric representation models.

1\. Mixture-of-experts (MoE) layers, including space-MoE and time-MoE layers, which enable the model to have billions of diffusion paths from the input text to the output image.  
2\. Each diffusion path acts as a "painter" that depicts a particular textual concept onto a specific region of the image at a given diffusion timestep.

Cones: Concept Neurons in Diffusion Models for Customized Generation  
Zhiheng Liu \+8  
International Conference on Machine Learning  
2023 ·  
95 citations  
DOI

1\. Identification of "concept neurons" in diffusion models, which are a small cluster of neurons that correspond to a particular subject. These concept neurons are identified using statistics of network gradients in response to stimuli related to the given subject.  
2\. Manipulation of image generation by shutting down the concept neurons to yield a particular subject in different contexts, or by concatenating multiple clusters of concept neurons to generate multiple related concepts in a single image.

Waterpixels  
V. Machairas \+5  
IEEE Transactions on Image Processing  
2015 ·  
94 citations  
DOI

The key algorithm introduced in this study is the "waterpixels" algorithm, which is a method for generating superpixels (homogeneous regions) from an image. The waterpixels algorithm is based on the marker-controlled watershed transformation and introduces a spatially regularized gradient to control the tradeoff between superpixel regularity and adherence to object boundaries. The algorithm has a linear time complexity with respect to the number of image pixels.

Making LLaMA SEE and Draw with SEED Tokenizer  
Yuying Ge \+6  
International Conference on Learning Representations  
2023 ·  
85 citations  
DOI

The key algorithms introduced in this paper are the SEED tokenizer and the SEED-LLaMA model. The SEED tokenizer is a novel image tokenizer designed to enable large language models (LLMs) to both comprehend and generate images, by representing images with 1D tokens that capture high-level semantics. The SEED-LLaMA model is an LLM that can perform multimodal tasks like comprehending and generating images, in addition to its original text-based capabilities, by using the SEED tokens.

Gradient-Based Synthesized Multiple Exposure Time Color HDR Image  
A. Várkonyi-Kóczy \+2  
IEEE Transactions on Instrumentation and Measurement  
2008 ·  
53 citations  
DOI

The key algorithm introduced in this study is a new tone reproduction algorithm for creating high dynamic range (HDR) color images. The algorithm synthesizes an HDR image by combining multiple exposures, but it does this separately for the red, green, and blue color channels before blending the modified color components together to produce a high-quality HDR color image that preserves details and color information even in scenes with a high dynamic range of illumination.

ExpoBlend: Information preserving exposure blending based on normalized log-domain entropy  
Neil D. B. Bruce  
Computers & graphics  
2014 ·  
52 citations  
DOI

The key algorithm introduced in this paper is the "ExpoBlend" algorithm, which performs HDR compression of multiple exposures while preserving image structure, details, and lighting, and allows adjusting the balance between illumination and fine details using a single parameter. The algorithm computes local entropy in a logarithmically compressed domain and uses a cross-exposure normalization and fusion strategy based on relative entropy.

An optimization-based approach to fusion of multi-exposure, low dynamic range images  
Ketan Kotwal \+1  
Fusion  
2011 ·  
25 citations

The key algorithm introduced in this paper is an optimization-based approach to fusing multiple low dynamic range (LDR) images captured at different exposures into a single high-quality fused LDR image. The algorithm formulates the image matting process as a multi-objective optimization problem and solves it using an Euler-Lagrange technique, producing fused images with high contrast without the need for an intermediate HDR image and tone mapping.

A Survey on Super-Resolution Methods for Image Reconstruction  
E. Karimi \+2  
2014 ·  
16 citations  
PDF  
DOI

1\) Frequency-domain methods: Tsai and Huang method, Taylor series expansion method, Recursive least squares method, Recursive Total Least Squares method, and Multi-channel sampling theorem method.

2\) Spatial-domain methods: Maximum likelihood (ML) estimator, Maximum a posteriori (MAP) methods using Gaussian Markov Random Field (GMRF), Huber MRF (HMRF), and Total Variation (TV) priors, Joint MAP restoration method, Bayes theory-based method, Example-based methods, Projection onto convex sets (POCS) methods, Adaptive filter-based methods, and Neural network-based methods.

3\) Wavelet-domain methods: The paper does not go into detail on specific wavelet-domain super-resolution algorithms, but states that several methods have been proposed in this domain.

Degeneration-Tuning: Using Scrambled Grid shield Unwanted Concepts from Stable Diffusion  
Zixuan Ni \+5  
ACM Multimedia  
2023 ·  
12 citations  
PDF  
DOI

1\. Denoising Diffusion Probabilistic Model (DDPM), Denoising Diffusion Implicit Model (DDIM), and score-based diffusion, which are recent advances in diffusion models that the paper builds upon.  
2\. Latent Diffusion Model (LDM), which uses pre-trained autoencoders like VAEs to encode images into a latent space.  
3\. The novel Degeneration Tuning (DT) method, which uses a Scrambled Grid operation to disrupt the low-frequency visual content of unwanted concepts, and then retrains the Stable Diffusion model on this degraded dataset.

SURVEY OF SUPER RESOLUTION TECHNIQUES  
Anand Deshpande \+1  
ICTACT Journal on Image and Video Processing  
2019 ·  
8 citations  
PDF  
DOI

1\. Frequency domain approaches such as the Tsai and Huang DFT-based method

3\. Interpolation-based approaches such as nearest neighbor, bilinear, and bicubic interpolation  
4\. Reconstruction-based approaches, both deterministic (using priors and regularization) and stochastic (using statistical estimation)  
5\. Learning-based approaches that use a database of example image patches to reconstruct the high-resolution output

Single image super-resolution with denoising diffusion GANS  
Heng Xiao \+6  
Scientific Reports  
2024 ·  
8 citations  
PDF  
DOI

1\. SRDDGAN (Single Image Super-Resolution with Denoising Diffusion GANS): A new algorithm that combines denoising diffusion models with GANs to generate high-resolution images, with the added benefit of large-step denoising, sample diversity, and training stability.  
2\. Latent variable Z: The SRDDGAN algorithm uses a latent variable Z to explore the diversity of likely high-resolution spatial domains.

Efficient Real-world Image Super-Resolution Via Adaptive Directional Gradient Convolution  
Long Peng \+7  
arXiv.org  
2024 ·  
7 citations  
DOI

1\. Adaptive Directional Gradient Convolution (DGConv) \- Uses kernel-wise differential operations and learnable directional gradient convolutions to adaptively fuse directional gradients and improve perception of gradient arrangements.  
2\. Equivalent parameter fusion method for DGConv \- Maintains the representational capabilities of DGConv while keeping computational costs consistent with a standard convolution.  
3\. Adaptive Information Interaction Block (AIIBlock) \- Balances enhancement of texture and contrast while investigating interdependencies.  
4\. DGPNet architecture \- Integrates the DGConv and AIIBlock components for real-world super-resolution.

SN Computer Science  
2021 ·  
6 citations  
PDF  
DOI

The key algorithm introduced and used in this study is the Savitzky-Golay parametric filtering approach for fusing multiple exposure images to generate an HDR image. This approach is used to generate alpha matte coefficients that help preserve weak edges and fine textures that would otherwise be lost in the fusion process.

Detail Enhanced Multi-Exposure Image Fusion Based On Edge Preserving Filters  
Harbinder Singh  
2018 ·  
6 citations  
DOI

1\. A novel multi-exposure image fusion approach based on texture features and nonlinear diffusion filters using partial differential equations (PDEs) to preserve edges and smooth regions.  
2\. Decomposition of multi-exposure images into base layers (BLs) and detail layers (DLs) to extract sharp and fine details.  
3\. Fusion of the BLs and DLs across the multi-exposure images using a Laplacian pyramid and edge-preserving filters to enhance texture details.  
4\. A novel exposure fusion technique using a weighted least squares (WLS) optimization framework to refine weight maps for the BLs and DLs, leading to a weighted average fusion approach.

Mohit Kumar \+1  
IEEE Transactions on Artificial Intelligence  
2023 ·  
4 citations  
DOI

1\. Multilevel superpixel-based classification, where the image is divided into a predetermined number of superpixels and then classified into under-exposed, well-exposed, and over-exposed regions based on superpixel contrast, entropy, and illumination statistics.  
2\. Support vector machine (SVM) classifier, which is trained on the consistently classified superpixel regions from the multilevel classification and then used to classify any remaining ambiguous regions.

SuperInpaint: Learning Detail-Enhanced Attentional Implicit Representation for Super-resolutional Image Inpainting  
Canyu Zhang \+6  
arXiv.org  
2023 ·  
3 citations  
DOI

1\. The "SuperInpaint" task, which involves reconstructing missing regions in low-resolution images and generating completed images at higher resolutions.  
2\. The "detail-enhanced attentional implicit representation (DEAR)" model, which is designed to address the SuperInpaint task. The DEAR model includes:  
\- A deep convolutional network to extract latent embeddings  
\- An adaptive high-pass filter to enhance high-frequency details  
\- An "unmask-attentional module" to suppress embeddings from masked pixels  
\- An importance map extraction module  
\- An implicit representation module that uses the detail-enhanced and unmask-attentional embeddings, importance values, and spatial distances to reconstruct the missing pixels

1\. PSO-CIQ: A combination of the particle swarm optimization (PSO) algorithm and the K-means clustering algorithm for color image quantization.

3\. SP-PSO-CIQ and SP-IDE-PSO-CIQ: Superpixel versions of the PSO-CIQ and IDE-PSO-CIQ algorithms, respectively.

Multi-exposure Fusion With JPEG Compression Guidance  
Xingdi Zhang \+3  
Visual Communications and Image Processing  
2018 ·  
0 citations  
DOI

1\) A technique for fusing multiple LDR images of varying exposures into an HDR image, without going through the traditional HDR assembly step.  
2\) An algorithm that uses JPEG compression bits to select the good regions from the input LDR images for the fusion, instead of relying on complicated algorithms that calculate image low-level features.  
3\) An algorithm that extracts the JPEG coding bits from the intermediate JPEG product, and uses these bits as weights for the exposure fusion, where well-exposed regions have higher bits and over/underexposed regions have lower bits.

2018 ·  
0 citations

1\) A new method for improving multiple-exposure combination for HDR imaging that compensates for violations of common assumptions in existing approaches.

3\) The tone-mapped versions of the HDR images produced by the new method do not exhibit hue shifts, color artifacts, or contrast problems that commonly occur with other multiple-exposure HDR approaches.

17 SreeRamaVamsidhar \+2  
arXiv.org  
2024 ·  
0 citations  
DOI

1\) A novel ISR algorithm that reformulates the task from generating super-resolved images to computing the inverse of the degradation kernels.  
2\) A technique called "Deep Identity Learning" which exploits the identity relation between the degradation and inverse degradation models.  
3\) The NSSR-DIL algorithm, which is computationally efficient, requiring an order of magnitude fewer resources than existing methods, while still achieving competitive performance, and is scale-invariant, not requiring retraining for different upscaling factors.

1\. Generative Adversarial Networks (GANs): A generative model that includes a generator network to create images and a discriminator network to evaluate the authenticity of the generated images. The two networks are trained in an adversarial process.

2\. Pixel-to-Pixel (Pix2Pix) image translation model: A specialized GAN-based model for image-to-image translation tasks. It uses a U-Net architecture and combines adversarial loss with L1 loss to preserve structural and semantic features during image translation.
